| TC-040 (data_edge) | Make Repayment Transaction_Amount entered with higher-than-supported decimal precision | A loan exists in 'Active' status with an amount due prefilled for repayment, The Make Repayment action is available | 1. Click 'Confirm' to submit the repayment | Form accepts the input; the saved transaction displays the Transaction_Amount rounded to the system's monetary precision on the Transactions table and in the loan balance (repayment succeeds and the displayed amount shows the rounded value) | low |

In the Entry Lines section add balanced lines: select <GL_Account> and 'Debit' with <Amount>, click 'Add Row', select <GL_Account> and 'Credit' with the same <Amount><br>8. Click the 'Create Journal Entry' button | A new row appears in the Journal Entries table with the entered <Office> and <Transaction_Date_After_Closing> (showing the journal entry was accepted because the date is after the closing date) | medium |

| TC-016 (boundary) | Attempt to select multiple Debit accounts while 'Allow Multiple Debit Entries' is unchecked | Create Rule form is available via "+ Create Rule", Debit_Account_or_Tag component supports multi-select and the form contains the Allow_Multiple_Debit_Entries checkbox | 1. Click the "+ Create Rule" button<br>2. Ensure the Allow_Multiple_Debit_Entries checkbox is unchecked<br>3. In Debit_Account_or_Tag, select one GL account/tag<br>4. Attempt to select a second GL account/tag in Debit_Account_or_Tag | Selection of a second debit account is blocked by the UI: when Allow_Multiple_Debit_Entries is unchecked the UI prevents choosing more than one debit account (the second selection is not applied) or an immediate inline control-level message appears preventing a multi-selection; in either case submission with multiple debit accounts is blocked | medium |
| TC-017 (input_edge) | Create Rule with a very long Rule_Name (200+ characters) | Create Rule form is available via "+ Create Rule" | 1. Click the "+ Create Rule" button<br>2. Enter a very long string (200+ characters) into the Rule_Name field<br>3. Fill any other required fields (if required) with valid selections<br>4. Click the "Create Rule" button | Form submits successfully; the rule is created and the Rule Detail view opens (creation succeeds). | TC-018 (input_edge) | Create Rule with Rule_Name containing leading and trailing whitespace | Create Rule form is available via "+ Create Rule" | 1. Click the "+ Create Rule" button<br>2. | TC-019 (interaction_edge) | Rapid double-click on Create Rule results in a single created rule (no duplicates) | Create Rule form is available and other required fields can be completed | 1. Click the "+ Create Rule" button<br>2. Fill Rule_Name and any required fields with valid values<br>3. Rapidly double-click the "Create Rule" button (two quick clicks)<br>4. After submit completes, navigate to Accounting_Rules_Table | Creation succeeds once: a single new rule row is created in Accounting_Rules_Table (only one record appears), and the UI does not show duplicate rows; any second submission attempt is blocked by the UI or ignored so no duplicate entity is created | medium |
| TC-020 (boundary) | Create Rule with Office left blank to apply rule to all offices | Create Rule form is available via "+ Create Rule", Office dropdown is present with the possibility to leave it blank | 1. | TC ID | Test Case | Preconditions | Steps | Expected Result | Priority |
|-------|-----------|---------------|-------|-----------------|----------|

| TC-014 (boundary) | Date_From one day after Date_To is blocked | User is on the Reports page, A report row is available | 1. Click the 'Run Report' button | Run Report is blocked; an inline validation error is shown on Date_From or Date_To indicating the start date cannot be after the end date (visible next to the date field) and no Generated_Report_Table is shown | medium |
| TC-015 (data_edge) | Far-future Date_From is accepted or handled without validation error | User is on the Reports page, A report row is available | 1. Click the report row's 'Open Parameters' action to open Parameters_Form<br>2. Enter <far future date> in Date_From<br>3. Optionally enter <far future date> or leave Date_To blank<br>4. Click the 'Run Report' button | Run Report succeeds; Generated_Report_Table is displayed (may be empty) and no date validation error is shown for the far-future date | medium |
| TC-016 (input_edge) | Run Report with both Date_From and Date_To left blank | User is on the Reports page, A report row is available | 1. Click the report row's 'Open Parameters' action to open Parameters_Form<br>2. Leave Date_From blank<br>3. Leave Date_To blank<br>4. Click the 'Run Report' button | Run Report succeeds; Generated_Report_Table is displayed (may contain full result set or be empty) and no date-related validation error is shown | low |
| TC-017 (interaction_edge) | Rapid double-click on 'Run Report' should not produce duplicate tables or duplicate processing | User is on the Reports page, Parameters_Form is open for a selected report | 1. Ensure Date_From/Date_To (or other parameters) are set or left blank per test intent<br>2. Double-click the 'Run Report' button quickly (two clicks within a short interval) | Only one Run Report action is processed; a single Generated_Report_Table appears with sorting and pagination controls (no duplicate tables or duplicate result blocks are shown) and any second click is ignored or the button becomes disabled while processing | medium |
| TC-018 (interaction_edge) | Rapid double-click on 'Export to Excel' should initiate only one download | User has successfully run a report and Generated_Report_Table is visible | 1. Click or focus the Generated_Report_Table's 'Export to Excel' action<br>2. Double-click the 'Export to Excel' action quickly (two clicks within a short interval) | Only one Excel download is initiated; the UI shows a single download action (the second click is ignored or the export button is disabled) and no duplicate download prompts appear | medium |
| TC-019 (interaction_edge) | Pressing browser Back immediately after running report returns to blank Parameters_Form and does not auto-create duplicates | User is on the Reports page, Parameters_Form is open and Run Report has been clicked successfully resulting in Generated_Report_Table | 1. After Generated_Report_Table is displayed, press the browser Back button once | Browser Back returns the user to the Parameters_Form and the form fields are blank (no residual selections); no additional Generated_Report_Table is automatically created by navigating back and there is no duplicate report processing triggered | medium |

Observe current state of Start/Stop Scheduler (on or off)<br>2. Rapidly toggle Start/Stop Scheduler off then on (or on then off) with two quick clicks<br>3. Observe the global control state and any changes to job scheduling indicators (Next_Run_Time / Currently_Running) | Final global scheduler state matches the last toggle action; no duplicate scheduler instances or duplicate scheduled executions are created as a result of rapid toggling; UI shows a consistent scheduler state (action succeeds) | medium |
| TC-028 (boundary) | Attempt to reorder code-list entries when only one entry exists is blocked | User can open a Code List from Manage Codes Table, Selected Code List has exactly one entry | 1. Open Manage Codes page<br>2. Click the row to open the Code_List_Detail for a code list that has exactly one entry<br>3. Click Reorder_Entries action | Reorder control is disabled or the action is blocked with a visible message indicating at least two entries are required to reorder (is blocked / error shown) | low |

## Logout

Total: **12** (positive: 5, negative: 4, edge: 0)

### Positive Tests

| TC ID | Test Case | Preconditions | Steps | Expected Result | Priority |
|-------|-----------|---------------|-------|-----------------|----------|
| TC-001 | Open Profile dropdown shows Profile Settings and Log Out | User logged in as <User> | 1. Click the <User Profile> icon in the top-right corner | Profile dropdown is displayed showing the 'Profile Settings' link and the 'Log Out' button | medium |
| TC-002 | Navigate to Profile Settings from Profile dropdown | User logged in as <User> | 1. Click the <User Profile> icon in the top-right corner to open the dropdown<br>2. Click the 'Profile Settings' item in the dropdown | The application navigates to the Profile Settings page; the Profile Settings page is displayed | medium |
| TC-003 | Log out via Profile dropdown redirects to Login page | User logged in as <User> | 1. Click the <User Profile> icon in the top-right corner to open the dropdown<br>2. Click the 'Log Out' button in the dropdown | User is redirected to the Login page and the Login form is visible | high |
| TC-004 | After logout, attempt to open an authenticated page redirects to Login page | User logged in as <User> | 1. Click the <User Profile> icon in the top-right corner to open the dropdown<br>2. Click the 'Log Out' button in the dropdown<br>3. Attempt to navigate to an authenticated page by entering the <authenticated route> in the browser address bar or clicking a bookmark to an authenticated page | Attempt to access the authenticated page is intercepted and the user is redirected to the Login page; the Login form is visible | high |
| TC-005 | Profile dropdown toggles closed when Profile icon clicked again | User logged in as <User> | 1. Click the <User Profile> icon in the top-right corner to open the dropdown<br>2. Click the <User Profile> icon again | Profile dropdown is no longer visible | low |

### Negative Tests

| TC ID | Test Case | Preconditions | Steps | Expected Result | Priority |
|-------|-----------|---------------|-------|-----------------|----------|
| TC-006 | Unauthenticated user tries to access an authenticated route | User is not authenticated | 1. Ensure the user is logged out / not authenticated<br>2. In the browser address bar, navigate to <authenticated page URL> | The Authenticated_Route_Guard triggers: the browser is redirected to the login page; the authenticated page content is not displayed and the URL changes to the login page (i.e., access is blocked) | high |
| TC-007 | Profile icon and Log Out are not available when user is logged out | User is not authenticated | 1. Ensure the user is logged out / not authenticated<br>2. Open the application landing page / main UI | User_Profile_Icon is not visible on the page; Profile_Dropdown is not accessible and the 'Log Out' item is not present (user cannot access logout when not logged in) | high |
| TC-008 | Direct attempt to invoke logout action while not authenticated is blocked | User is not authenticated | 1. Ensure the user is logged out / not authenticated<br>2. In the browser address bar, navigate directly to <logout action URL> and press Enter | The logout precondition ('user must be logged in') fails and the request is blocked: the browser is redirected to the login page; no logout flow is performed and no authenticated session is terminated (i.e., logout action cannot be executed by unauthenticated user) | high |
| TC-009 | After logging out, navigating back to a protected page is blocked | User is authenticated at test start | 1. Log in as a valid user and verify authenticated UI is shown<br>2. Click User_Profile_Icon<br>3. Click 'Log Out' in the Profile_Dropdown<br>4. After logout completes and the login page is shown, use the browser Back button or navigate to <previous authenticated page URL> | Authenticated route guard redirects the browser to the login page; the previously authenticated page content is not restored and no authenticated content is visible (access after logout is blocked) | high |

### Edge & Boundary Tests

| TC ID | Test Case | Preconditions | Steps | Expected Result | Priority |
|-------|-----------|---------------|-------|-----------------|----------|
| TC-010 (interaction_edge) | Rapid double-click of 'Log Out' button | user is logged in, User_Profile_Icon is visible, Profile_Dropdown is visible after clicking User_Profile_Icon | 1. Click User_Profile_Icon to open Profile_Dropdown<br>2. Rapidly double-click the 'Log Out' button (two clicks within 300ms) | Single logout action succeeds: the app performs one session termination and redirects to the login page once; authentication token is cleared; no error message is shown; User_Profile_Icon and Profile_Dropdown are not visible after redirect. | medium |
| TC-011 (state_edge) | Click 'Log Out' then immediately click 'Profile Settings' in the dropdown | user is logged in, User_Profile_Icon is visible, Profile_Dropdown is visible after clicking User_Profile_Icon | 1. Click User_Profile_Icon to open Profile_Dropdown<br>2. Click 'Log Out' once<br>3. Immediately (before redirect finishes) click 'Profile Settings' in the same Profile_Dropdown | Navigation to Profile Settings is blocked; the logout action still succeeds and the app redirects to the login page; Profile Settings page is not displayed and the Profile_Dropdown is not accessible after redirect. | medium |
| TC-012 (interaction_edge) | Use browser Back after logout to reach an authenticated page | user is logged in, User_Profile_Icon is visible | 1. Click User_Profile_Icon to open Profile_Dropdown<br>2. Click 'Log Out' once and confirm redirect to login page<br>3. Press the browser Back button to navigate to the previously viewed authenticated page | Attempt to navigate back to an authenticated page is blocked by the Authenticated_Route_Guard; the user is redirected to the login page; authentication token remains cleared; User_Profile_Icon is not visible on the resulting page. | medium |
